app.factory("uiErrorService", ["$http", "messageService", function() {
    var n = {};
    return n.setControlErrors = function(n) {
        var t, i;
        if (n != null)
            for (t = 0; t < n.length; t++)
                i = $("#" + n[t].Key),
                i.length || (i = $("[name=" + n[t].Key.replace("References", "referencePerson").replace("[", "\\[").replace("]", "\\]").replace(".", "\\.") + "]")),
                i.addClass("input-validation-error"),
                $("<span class='field-validation-error' data-valmsg-for='" + n[t].Key + "' + data-valmsg-replace='true'><\/span>").html(n[t].Value[0]).appendTo(i.parent())
    }
    ,
    n.removeControlErrors = function() {
        $(".input-validation-error").removeClass("input-validation-error");
        $("span.field-validation-error").remove()
    }
    ,
    n.resetControlErrors = function(t) {
        var i, r;
        if (n.removeControlErrors(),
        t != null)
            for (i = 0; i < t.length; i++)
                r = $("#" + t[i].Key),
                r.length || (r = $("[name='" + t[i].Key.replace("References", "referencePerson").replace("[", "\\[").replace("]", "\\]").replace(".", "\\.") + "']")),
                r.addClass("input-validation-error"),
                $("<span class='field-validation-error' data-valmsg-for='" + t[i].Key + "' + data-valmsg-replace='true'><\/span>").html(t[i].Value[0]).appendTo(r.parent())
    }
    ,
    n
}

    }

    }

    n.save = function(i, r) {
        if (n.isPerformingServerAction === !1) {
            n.VA.StatusScan = n.currentStatus;
            n.VA.StatusScan == v.WARNING && (n.VA.Overwritten === !0 && (n.VA.Overwritten = !1),
            n.VA.Ignored === !0 && (n.VA.Ignored = !1));
            n.VA.OnlyNationals = n.SetOnlyNationals();
            n.isPerformingServerAction = !0;
            n.SuccessMessage = "";
            n.ErrorMessage = "";
            n.Errors = [];
            n.VA.Confirm_Email = n.confirmEmail;
            s.removeControlErrors();
            n.VA.ClientDateTime = u("date")(new Date, "dd/MM/yyyy HH:mm:ss");
            n.VA.Application_AddComment != null && (n.VA.Application_Comment = n.escapeHtml(n.VA.Application_Comment));
            var e = !0;
            i == "Submit" && $("input[data-val-phonenumber]").each(function(t, i) {
                var r, u;
                if ($(i).val() != null && $(i).val() != undefined && $(i).val() != "") {
                    r = !0;
                    try {
                        u = $(i).val();
                        r = libphonenumber.isValidPhoneNumber(u)
                    } catch (f) {
                        r = !1
                    }
                    r == !1 && (n.Errors.push({
                        Key: $(i).attr("id"),
                        Value: [$(i).attr("data-val-phonenumber")]
                    }),
                    e = !1,
                    n.VA.PhoneValid = e)
                }
            });
            t({
                method: "POST",
                url: "/VisaApplication/" + i,
                data: $.param(n.VA),
                headers: {
                    "Content-Type": "application/x-www-form-urlencoded"
                }
            }).success(function(t) {
                var o, l, h, c, u, y, p;
                if (t.Success === !1) {
                    if (e)
                        n.Errors = t.ModelErrors;
                    else {
                        if (o = [],
                        t.ModelErrors !== undefined && t.ModelErrors !== null)
                            for (u = 0; u < t.ModelErrors.length; u++) {
                                for (l = t.ModelErrors[u],
                                h = 0; h < n.Errors.length; h++)
                                    c = n.Errors[h],
                                    c.Value[0].indexOf(l.Value[0].substring(0, 4)) >= 0 && !c.handled && (o.push(c),
                                    n.Errors[h].handled = !0);
                                o.push(t.ModelErrors[u])
                            }
                        for (u = 0; u < n.Errors.length; u++)
                            n.Errors[u].handled || o.push(n.Errors[u]);
                        n.Errors = o
                    }
                    s.setControlErrors(n.Errors);
                    $(".back-to-top").triggerHandler("click")
                } else
                    i == "Submit" && (location.href = location.href),
                    i === "AddApplicationToTheJourney" ? f.location.href = "/" + f.location.pathname.replace(/^\/([^\/]*).*$/, "$1") + "/VisaApplication/Edit/" + t.VA.AppId : (n.SuccessMessage = t.SuccessMessage,
                    n.VA = t.VA,
                    n.AppointmentTaken = n.VA.SubGroupId !== undefined && n.VA.SubGroupId !== null,
                    n.VA.SelectedVacCountry == null && (n.VA.SelectedVacCountry = undefined),
                    r != null && (n.VA.StatusId = r),
                    i == "UpdateApplicationDate" && (y = "/" + f.location.pathname.replace(/^\/([^\/]*).*$/, "$1") + "nl/VisaApplication/PrintVA?AppId=" + n.AppId + "&PrintLanguage=en-US",
                    p = window.open(y, "_blank"),
                    p.focus()),
                    n.setsexValue(),
                    n.initializeApplication(t),
                    n.currentStatus = n.VA.StatusScan,
                    a.sendSuccessMessage(t.SuccessMessage));
                typeof t.rights != "undefined" && t.rights && (n.rights = t.rights);
                n.isPerformingServerAction = !1;
                n.MrzCheckBoxChecked = !1;
                n.checkBoxIgnored = n.VA.StatusScan == v.NOSCAN || n.VA.StatusScan == v.WARNING;
                n.ArrowShow = n.VA.StatusScan == v.WARNING;
                n.InitializeMrz();
                n.isPermitForResidenceRequired();
                n.isPermitForDestinationRequired()
            }).error(function() {
                n.Errors = [];
                n.ErrorMessage = "Unexpected Error";
                n.isPerformingServerAction = !1
            })
        }
    }

    }

    }

    function a(n) {
        if (n !== undefined && n.Value[0] !== undefined)
            return '<table cellpadding="5" cellspacing="0" border="0" style="padding-left:50px;"><tr><td style="color:red;"><b>ERROR:<\/b>' + n.Value[0] + "<\/td><\/tr><\/table>"
    }

    }

    }

    }

    }

            n.listData[i].Id === t && n.listData.splice(i, 1);
        o.fnClearTable();
        n.listData.length > 0 && o.fnAddData(n.listData)
    }
    ;

        aLengthMenu: [[-1, 10, 25, 50, 100], ["All", 10, 25, 50, 100]],

    n.scan = function() {

        n.Errors = [],
        e.removeControlErrors(),
        t({
            method: "POST",
            url: "/ReceiveDocument/Scan",
            params: {
                ReferenceNumber: n.ReferenceNumber
            },
            headers: {
                "Content-Type": "application/x-www-form-urlencoded"
            }
        }).success(function(t) {
            if (t.Success === !1)

            else {

                    for (var i = n.listData.length - 1; i >= 0; i--)
                        n.listData[i].Id === t.VA.Id && (n.DoubleScan = !0);

            n.Errors = [];

            n.isPerformingServerAction = !1
        }));

    }
    ;

            n.applicationList = [];

                n.applicationList.push(t.Id)
            });
            var i = n.applicationList;
            n.SuccessMessage = "";
            n.ErrorMessage = "";
            n.Errors = [];

                method: "POST",
                url: "/ReceiveDocument/Save",
                data: {
                    applications: i
                },
                dataType: "json",
                traditional: !0
            }).success(function(t) {
                var i, f, r;
                if (t.Success === !1) {
                    for (n.Errors = t.ModelErrors,
                    i = n.listData.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
                        if (f = !0,
                        n.Errors != null)
                            for (r = n.Errors.length - 1; r >= 0; r--)
                                n.listData[i].Id === n.Errors[r].Key && (f = !1);
                        f && n.removeVA(n.listData[i].Id)
                    }
                    angular.forEach(n.listData, function(t) {
                        var i, r, u;
                        if (n.Errors != null)
                            for (i = 0; i <= n.Errors.length - 1; i++)
                                t.Id === n.Errors[i].Key && (r = $("#" + t.Id),
                                u = o.api().row(r),
                                u.child(a(n.Errors[i])).show(),
                                r.addClass("shown"))
                    });
                    $(".back-to-top").triggerHandler("click")
                } else
                    u.sendSuccessMessage(t.SuccessMessage),
                    n.listData = [],
                    o.fnClearTable();
                n.isPerformingServerAction = !1
            }).error(function() {
                n.Errors = [];
                n.ErrorMessage = "Unexpected Error";
                n.isPerformingServerAction = !1
            })
        }
    }
}

    }

          , r = $("input[type=checkbox]").is(":checked")
          , i = $("input[type=checkbox]:checked").length;

    }
    ;

                for (j = 0; j < n.ListOfApplicationsByGroup[i].VisaGroupInfos.length; j++)
                    n.ListOfApplicationsByGroup[i].VisaGroupInfos[j].StatusId != 1 && n.ListOfApplicationsByGroup[i].VisaGroupInfos[j].IntendedDateOfArrivalInTheFuture && (n.ListOfApplicationsByGroup[i].VisaGroupInfos[j].Selected = n.AllSelected)
    }

                groupId: i
            }
        }).success(function(t) {

        })
    }

                vacoreId: i
            }
        }).success(function(t) {
            t.Success === !0 ? (n.ListOfApplicationsByGroup = t.list,
            n.MakeAppointmentDisabled = t.MakeAppointmentDisabled,

    }

    }

      , f = angular.element(document.querySelector("#longStay")).val();

        Value: 0,
        Text: "-"
    }, {
        Value: 1,

    }, {

        Text: f
    }];
    n.GDPR.visaTypeSelected = 0;
    n.gdprApproval = !1;
    n.showErrorGdprApproval = !1;
    n.ShowErrorNoSelection = !1;
    n.gdprLink = function(t) {
        n.ActivateCaptcha = t;
        n.GdprApprovalChexBoxShow = !0;
        n.showErrorGdprPleaseRead = !1;
        n.ShowErrorNoSelection = !1
    }
    ;
    n.visaTypeChange = function() {
        n.GdprApprovalChexBoxShow = !1;
        n.showErrorGdprApproval = !1;
        n.showErrorNoSelection = !1;
        n.showErrorGdprPleaseRead = !1;
        n.gdprApproval = !1;
        $("#GdprApproval").prop("checked", !1)
    }
    ;
    n.gdprApprove = function() {
        var i, u;
        n.vaCoreId;
        n.gdprApproval === !0 ? (n.showErrorGdprApproval = !1,
        n.ShowErrorNoSelection = !1,
        n.path = r.location.origin + r.location.pathname.replace("Gdpr", "CreateGdprNewWithAutoNumber"),
        i = "",
        n.ActivateCaptcha === !0 && (i = document.querySelector("iframe[data-hcaptcha-response]").getAttribute("data-hcaptcha-response")),
        u = {
            Approval: n.GDPR.visaTypeSelected,
            RecaptchaResponse: i
        },
        n.ErrorMessage = "",
        t({
            method: "POST",
            url: n.path,
            data: $.param(u),
            headers: {
                "Content-Type": "application/x-www-form-urlencoded"
            }
        }).success(function(t) {
            t.Success === !1 ? n.ErrorMessage = t.ErrorMessage : (n.vaCoreId = t.VACoreId,
            n.path = r.location.origin + r.location.pathname.replace("Gdpr", "Edit") + "/" + t.VACoreId,
            r.location.href = n.path)
        }).error(function() {
            n.ErrorMessage = "Err"
        })) : n.GDPR.visaTypeSelected == null || n.GDPR.visaTypeSelected === 0 ? (n.showErrorNoSelection = !0,
        n.showErrorGdprApproval = !1) : (r.location.href = "#rgbdError",
        n.showErrorGdprApproval = !0,
        n.GdprApprovalChexBoxShow == !1 ? (n.showErrorGdprPleaseRead = !0,
        n.showErrorGdprApproval = !1) : (n.showErrorGdprApproval = !0,
        n.showErrorGdprPleaseRead = !1),
        n.showErrorNoSelection = !1)
    }
    ;
    n.gdprCancel = function() {
        window.location = "/"
    }
}
